The user wants to fix a series of critical bugs and add usability features to their comprehensive HR management system. The key requirements are:
1.  **Fix Attendance & GPS System:** The core issue is the attendance system. Users see Location must be enabled errors even when GPS is on. The system should also log and display which location was used for each punch. Buttons for check-in/out should be disabled outside of designated work hours.
2.  **Restore Employee Requests:** The Employee Requests feature (e.g., Forgot Punch) was accidentally removed from the attendance page and must be restored.
3.  **Improve UI/UX:** The user requested an improved UI for the attendance page and a fix for mobile responsiveness issues, specifically with notifications being hidden.
4.  **Enhance Transaction Management (for STAS):**
    *   Implement color-coding for transaction statuses: Green (Executed), Yellow (Pending), Red (Rejected).
    *   Implement a barcode-based signature system for STAS on transaction PDFs. The PDF should have two barcodes: one for the signature and another at the bottom with the transaction serial number for physical filing.
    *   Add a camera-based search feature for STAS and Sultan to scan the transaction barcode and instantly pull up the corresponding electronic record.
5.  **Fix Permissions & Access:**
    *   Sultan and STAS must have identical, unrestricted permissions, including full edit access to contracts and the ability to edit official holidays.
    *   Implement a feature to revert an active contract back to a draft state.
6.  **Fix Leave Balance Calculation:** Ensure the leave balance for migrated employees is calculated correctly based on their opening balance and hire date, not the start of the year.
7.  **Device Management:** The Registered Devices page needs to function correctly.
